                        <td>
                        <div id="helptitle_container" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1px; border-color: black; background-color: rgb(193, 218, 215); text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 10.24px;"><a href="https://www.instanttvchannel.com/helpnn" target="_blank" style="color: black; text-decoration: none;">Help:</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>
                        <div>Content Editor</div>
                        </div>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                        <td class="help" style="text-align: justify; font-size: 11.2px;">
                        <p>The Content Editor is used to edit the configuration data for content items, and to determine the channel layout. The Content Editor automatically stores this information in the&nbsp;<a href="https://www.instanttvchannel.com/helpnn/s3feed" target="_blank" style="color: black;">S3 channel feed files</a>.</p>
                        <p><b>Upper Left Window</b>&nbsp;- An editable tree diagram of the channel layout. From this window content items can be selected, added, copied, moved, or deleted. Left click a tree element to select it,&nbsp;<b>right click</b>&nbsp;to bring up a context menu. Drag and drop an item to move it.</p>
                        <p><b>Upper Right Window</b>&nbsp;- The selected item's poster or picture (png/jpg/gif) for its Parent List, Springboard, or Picture screen.</p>
                        <p><b>Lower Window</b>&nbsp;- The editable settings for the selected item. All items have a default value that should work well in most situations. Many of the items are&nbsp;<a href="http://sdkdocs.roku.com/display/sdkdoc/Content+Meta-Data" target="_blank" style="color: black;">Content Meta-Data Attributes</a>&nbsp;that are described in the Roku SDK Wiki.</p>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                </tbody>
            </table>
            </div>
            </td>
        </tr>
